## Introduction

Having proved a preservation property in the last chapter, a natural
next step would be to prove progress. That is, to prove a property
of the form

    If γ ⊢ M ↓ v, then either M is a lambda abstraction or M —→ N for some N.

Such a property would tell us that having a denotation implies either
reduction to normal form or divergence. This is indeed true, but we
can prove a much stronger property! In fact, having a denotation that
is a function value (not `⊥`) implies reduction to a lambda
abstraction.

This stronger property, reformulated a bit, is known as _adequacy_.
That is, if a term `M` is denotationally equal to a lambda abstraction,
then `M` reduces to a lambda abstraction.

    ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)  implies M —↠ ƛ N' for some N'

Recall that `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)` is equivalent to saying that `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦
w)` for some `v` and `w`. We will show that `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies
multi-step reduction a lambda abstraction.  The recursive structure of
the derivations for `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` are completely different from
the structure of multi-step reductions, so a direct proof would be
challenging. However, The structure of `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` closer to
that of [BigStep]({{ site.baseurl }}/BigStep/) call-by-name
evaluation. Further, we already proved that big-step evaluation
implies multi-step reduction to a lambda (`cbn→reduce`). So we shall
prove that `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c`, where `c` is a
closure (a term paired with an environment), `γ'` is an environment
that maps variables to closures, and `γ` and `γ'` are appropriate
related.  The proof will be an induction on the derivation of
`γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, and to strengthen the induction hypothesis, we will relate
semantic values to closures using a _logical relation_ `𝕍`.

The rest of this chapter is organized as follows.

* To make the `𝕍` relation down-closed with respect to `⊑`,
  we must loosen the requirement that `M` result in a function value and
  instead require that `M` result in a value that is greater than or
  equal to a function value. We establish several properties about
  being ``greater than a function''.

* We define the logical relation `𝕍` that relates values and closures,
  and extend it to a relation on terms `𝔼` and environments `𝔾`.
  We prove several lemmas that culminate in the property that
  if `𝕍 v c` and `v′ ⊑ v`, then `𝕍 v′ c`.

* We prove the main lemma,
  that if `𝔾 γ γ'` and `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, then `𝔼 v (clos M γ')`.

* We prove adequacy as a corollary to the main lemma.

<a id="3964" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3969" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="3976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">plfa.part3.Soundness</a> <a id="3997" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="4003" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4004" href="plfa.part3.Soundness.html#23358" class="Function">soundness</a><a id="4013" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}

## The property of being greater or equal to a function

We define the following short-hand for saying that a value is
greather-than or equal to a function value.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="above-fun"></a><a id="4190" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="4200" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4202" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4208" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4210" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="4214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="4224" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4224" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4226" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4228" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="4231" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4231" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4233" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="4235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4241" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">]</a> <a id="4243" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="4246" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4246" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4248" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="4250" href="plfa.part3.Denotational.html#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4256" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">]</a> <a id="4258" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4231" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4260" href="plfa.part3.Denotational.html#4183" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="4262" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4246" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4264" href="plfa.part3.Denotational.html#4508" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="4266" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4224" class="Bound">u</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
If a value `u` is greater than a function, then an even greater value `u'`
is too.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="above-fun-⊑"></a><a id="4361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4361" class="Function">above-fun-⊑</a> <a id="4373" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4375" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="4377" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4377" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4379" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4379" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="4382" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4384" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="4389" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="4397" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="4409" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4377" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4411" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4413" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4377" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4508" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="4417" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4379" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
        <a id="4428" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
      <a id="4454" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="4466" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4379" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
<a id="4469" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4361" class="Function">above-fun-⊑</a> <a id="4481" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4483" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4483" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4485" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4487" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4489" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4489" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4491" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4493" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4493" class="Bound">lt&#39;</a> <a id="4497" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4499" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4501" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4501" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="4504" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4506" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4508" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4483" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4510" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4512" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4514" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4489" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4516" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4798" class="InductiveConstructor">⊑-trans</a> <a id="4526" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4493" class="Bound">lt&#39;</a> <a id="4530" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4501" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="4533" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4535" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The bottom value `⊥` is not greater than a function.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="above-fun⊥"></a><a id="4600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4600" class="Function">above-fun⊥</a> <a id="4611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4613" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="4615" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="4625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4171" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="4627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4600" class="Function">above-fun⊥</a> <a id="4638" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4640" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4640" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="4642" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4644" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4646" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4646" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="4648" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4650" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4650" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="4653" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4655" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="4661" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="4666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#43091" class="Function">sub-inv-fun</a> <a id="4678" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4650" class="Bound">lt</a>
<a id="4681" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="4685" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="4687" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4689" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4691" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4693" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4695" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4695" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="4697" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4699" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4701" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4701" class="Bound">Γ⊆⊥</a> <a id="4705" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4707" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4709" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4709" class="Bound">lt1</a> <a id="4713" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4715" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4715" class="Bound">lt2</a> <a id="4719" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4721" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4723" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4725" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="4731" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="4736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#32284" class="Function">all-funs∈</a> <a id="4746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4695" class="Bound">f</a>
<a id="4748" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="4752" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="4754" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4756" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4756" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4758" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4760" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="4762" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4762" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="4764" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4766" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4766" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="4768" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="4770" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="4776" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="4781" class="Bound">Γ⊆⊥</a> <a id="4785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4766" class="Bound">m</a>
<a id="4787" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="4791" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="4793" class="Symbol">()</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
If the join of two values `u` and `u'` is greater than a function, then
at least one of them is too.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="above-fun-⊔"></a><a id="4907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4907" class="Function">above-fun-⊔</a> <a id="4919" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4921" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="4923" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4923" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4925" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4925" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="4927" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="4940" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="4952" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4953" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4923" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4213" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4957" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4925" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="4959" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="4972" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="4984" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4923" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4986" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Sum.Base.html#612" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="4988" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="4998" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4925" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

    <a id="5173" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="5178" class="Bound">Γ⊆u⊔u&#39;</a> <a id="5185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5163" class="Bound">m</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
On the other hand, if neither of `u` and `u'` is greater than a function,
then their join is also not greater than a function.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="not-above-fun-⊔"></a><a id="5412" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5412" class="Function">not-above-fun-⊔</a> <a id="5428" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5430" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5432" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5432" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5434" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5434" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5439" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5444" class="Symbol">}</a>
               <a id="5461" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5463" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5465" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="5475" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5432" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5477" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5479" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5481" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="5491" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5434" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
               <a id="5509" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5511" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5513" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="5523" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5524" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5432" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5526" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4213" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5528" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5434" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5530" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5532" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5412" class="Function">not-above-fun-⊔</a> <a id="5548" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5548" class="Bound">naf1</a> <a id="5553" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5553" class="Bound">naf2</a> <a id="5558" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5558" class="Bound">af12</a>
    <a id="5567" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="5572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4907" class="Function">above-fun-⊔</a> <a id="5584" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5558" class="Bound">af12</a>
<a id="5589" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5593" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5595" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Sum.Base.html#662" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="5600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5600" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5604" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5606" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#809" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5620" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5600" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="5624" class="Bound">naf1</a>
<a id="5629" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="5633" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="5635" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Sum.Base.html#687" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="5640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5640" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5644" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5646" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#809" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="5660" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5640" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="5664" class="Bound">naf2</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The converse is also true. If the join of two values is not above a
function, then neither of them is individually.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="not-above-fun-⊔-inv"></a><a id="5795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5795" class="Function">not-above-fun-⊔-inv</a> <a id="5815" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5817" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5819" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5819" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5821" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5821" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5824" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5831" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5833" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5835" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5837" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="5847" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5848" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5819" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5850" href="plfa.part3.Denotational.html#4213" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5852" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5821" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5854" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="5870" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5872" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="5884" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5819" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5886" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#1162" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="5888" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5890" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="5900" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#5821" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
The property of being greater than a function value is decidable, as
exhibited by the following function.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="above-fun?"></a><a id="6385" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6385" class="Function">above-fun?</a> <a id="6396" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6399" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#6399" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="6401" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6403" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="6408" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6410" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6412" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#605" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="6416" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6417" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="6427" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#6399" class="Bound">v</a><a id="6428" class="Symbol">)</a>

Operator">⟨</a> <a id="6606" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#6577" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="6608" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6610" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="6612" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#6583" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="6614" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor">⊑-conj-R1</a> <a id="6627" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#6587" class="Bound">lt</a><a id="6629" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6631" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" <a id="6635" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="6639" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6641" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="6654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6654" class="Bound">v</a> class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="6667" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="6669" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor class="Bound">w</a> <a id="6687" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% <a id="6704" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="6706" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}

## Relating values to closures

Next we relate semantic values to closures.  The relation `𝕍` is for
closures whose term is a lambda abstraction, i.e., in weak-head normal
form (WHNF). The relation 𝔼 is for any closure. Roughly speaking,
`𝔼 v c` will hold if, when `v` is greater than a function value, `c` evaluates
to a closure `c'` in WHNF and `𝕍 v c'`. Regarding `𝕍 v c`, it will hold when
`c` is in WHNF, and if `v` is a function, the body of `c` evaluates
according to `v`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝕍"></a><a id="7244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7246" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="7254" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7256" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2467" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7261" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7263" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="𝔼"></a><a id="7267" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7267" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="7269" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7271" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="7277" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2467" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7284" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7286" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
We define `𝕍` as a function from values and closures to `Set` and not as a
data type because it is mutually recursive with `𝔼` in a negative
position (to the left of an implication).  We first perform case
analysis on the term in the closure. If the term is a variable or
application, then `𝕍` is false (`Bot`). If the term is a lambda
abstraction, we define `𝕍` by recursion on the value, which we
describe below.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="7715" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7717" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7717" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7719" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7725" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4330" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="7728" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7728" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7730" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7732" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7732" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7733" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7735" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7737" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.html#279" class="Datatype">Bot</a>
<a id="7741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7743" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7743" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7751" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7752" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7752" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="7756" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7756" class="Bound">M₁</a><a id="7758" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7760" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7760" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7761" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7763" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7765" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.html#279" class="Datatype">Bot</a>
<a id="7769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7771" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4171" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a> <a id="7773" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7779" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7782" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7782" class="Bound">M</a><a id="7783" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7785" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7785" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7786" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7788" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7790" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#137" class="Record">⊤</a>
<a id="7792" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7794" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7795" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7795" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7797" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4183" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="7799" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7799" class="Bound">w</a><a id="7800" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7802" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7803" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7808" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7811" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7811" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7812" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7814" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7814" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7815" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7817" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="7823" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="7826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7826" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7828" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7830" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2467" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="7834" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7836" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7838" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7267" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="7840" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7795" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7842" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7826" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7844" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7846" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="7856" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7799" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7858" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7860" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="7863" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7863" class="Bound">c&#39;</a> <a id="7866" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="7868" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#2467" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7873" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">]</a>
        <a id="7883" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7814" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="7886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2672" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="7889" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7826" class="Bound">c</a><a id="7890" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7892" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#3021" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7894" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7811" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="7896" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#3021" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="7898" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7863" class="Bound">c&#39;</a>  <a id="7902" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#1162" class="Function Operator">×</a>  <a id="7905" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7907" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7799" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7909" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7863" class="Bound">c&#39;</a><a id="7911" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7915" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7916" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7916" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="7918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4213" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="7920" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7920" class="Bound">v</a><a id="7921" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7923" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7929" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7930" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7932" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7932" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7933" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7935" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7935" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7936" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7938" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7940" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7942" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7916" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="7944" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7945" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7950" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7951" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7953" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7932" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7954" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7956" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7935" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7957" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7959" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#1162" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="7961" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7963" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7920" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7966" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7971" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7972" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7974" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7932" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7975" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7977" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7935" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7978" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
* If the value is `⊥`, then the result is true (`⊤`).

* If the value is a join (u ⊔ v), then the result is the pair
  (conjunction) of 𝕍 is true for both u and v.

* The important case is for a function value `v ↦ w` and closure
  `clos (ƛ N) γ`. Given any closure `c` such that `𝔼 v c`, if `w` is
  greater than a function, then `N` evaluates (with `γ` extended with `c`)
  to some closure `c'` and we have `𝕍 w c'`.


The definition of `𝔼` is straightforward. If `v` is a greater than a
function, then `M` evaluates to a closure related to `v`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="8538" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7267" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="8540" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8540" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8542" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8543" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="8548" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8548" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="8550" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8550" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="8552" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8554" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8556" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="8566" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8540" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8568" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8570" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="8573" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8573" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8575" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="8577" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#2467" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="8582" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">]</a> <a id="8584" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8550" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="8587" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#3021" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="8589" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8548" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="8591" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#3021" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="8593" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8573" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8595" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#1162" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="8597" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="8599" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8540" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8601" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8573" class="Bound">c</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The proof of the main lemma is by induction on `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, so it goes
underneath lambda abstractions and must therefore reason about open
terms (terms with variables). So we must relate environments of
semantic values to environments of closures.  In the following, `𝔾`
relates `γ` to `γ'` if the corresponding values and closures are related
by `𝔼`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝔾"></a><a id="8965" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8965" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="8967" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8969" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8971" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8971" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="8972" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8974" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7288" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="8980" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8971" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8982" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8984" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2437" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="8992" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8971" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8994" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8996" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="9000" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8965" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9002" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9003" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9003" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9004" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9006" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9006" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9008" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9008" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9011" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9013" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9015" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9015" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9017" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9019" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9003" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3521" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="9023" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9024" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9026" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9028" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7267" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="9030" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9031" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9006" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9033" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9015" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9034" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9036" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9037" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9008" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9040" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9015" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9041" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="𝔾-∅"></a><a id="9044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9044" class="Function">𝔾-∅</a> <a id="9048" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9050" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8965" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7412" class="Function">`∅</a> <a id="9055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2650" class="Function">∅&#39;</a>

<a id="𝔾-ext"></a><a id="9068" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9068" class="Function">𝔾-ext</a> <a id="9074" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9076" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9078" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9078" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9079" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9081" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9081" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9083" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7288" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="9089" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9078" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9090" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9092" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9092" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9095" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2437" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="9105" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9078" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9106" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9108" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9108" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9110" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9110" class="Bound">c</a><a id="9111" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="9119" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8965" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9123" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9081" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9125" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9092" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9128" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9130" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7267" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="9132" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9108" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9134" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9110" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9136" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9138" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#8965" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9140" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9141" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9081" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7445" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="9146" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9108" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9147" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9149" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9150" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9092" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2672" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="9156" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9110" class="Bound">c</a><a id="9157" class="Symbol">)</a>

We need a few properties of the `𝕍` and `𝔼` relations.  The first is that
a closure in the `𝕍` relation must be in weak-head normal form.  We
define WHNF has follows.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="9400" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="WHNF"></a><a id="9405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9405" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9410" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9412" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9414" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9415" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9415" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9417" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9417" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9418" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9420" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9422" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9415" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9426" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9417" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9428" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9430" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="9434" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="WHNF.ƛ_"></a><a id="9442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="9445" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9447" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9449" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9450" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9450" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9451" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9453" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9454" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9454" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="9456" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9458" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9450" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9460" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3191" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9462" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="9464" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9466" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9467" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="9474" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9405" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="9484" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9454" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9485" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The proof goes by cases on the term in the closure.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝕍→WHNF"></a><a id="9549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9549" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9556" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9558" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9560" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9560" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9561" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9563" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9563" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9565" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2437" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="9575" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9560" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9576" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9578" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9578" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9580" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9582" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9560" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9584" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9586" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9587" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9589" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9589" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9590" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="9599" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9603" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9589" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9611" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9578" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9613" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9563" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="9614" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9616" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9618" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9405" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9623" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9578" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="9625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9549" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9632" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9633" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9635" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4330" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="9639" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9639" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9640" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9642" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9643" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9643" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9644" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9646" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="9649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9549" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9656" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9657" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9659" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="9663" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9663" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9664" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9666" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9667" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9667" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9668" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9670" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9670" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="9673" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9675" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
Next we have an introduction rule for `𝕍` that mimics the `⊔-intro`
rule. If both `u` and `v` are related to a closure `c`, then their join is
too.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝕍⊔-intro"></a><a id="9862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9862" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="9871" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9873" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9875" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9875" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9877" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9877" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9879" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9879" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9880" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="9891" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9895" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9877" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9897" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9875" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9899" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9901" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9903" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9879" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9905" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9875" class="Bound">c</a>
           <a id="9918" class="Comment">---------------</a>
         <a id="9943" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9947" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9948" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9877" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4213" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9952" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9879" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9953" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9955" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9875" class="Bound">c</a>
<a id="9957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9862" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="9966" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9972" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9973" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4330" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="9975" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9975" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9976" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9978" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9978" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="9979" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9981" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="9984" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#9984" class="Bound">vc</a>
<a id="9987" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9862" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="9996" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10005" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10005" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10006" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10008" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10008" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10009" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10011" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10011" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="10014" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10014" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10017" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10019" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="10021" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10011" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="10024" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10026" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10014" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10029" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="10031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9862" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10040" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10046" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10047" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10047" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="10049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10051" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10051" class="Bound">M</a><a id="10052" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10054" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10054" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10055" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10057" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="10060" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10060" class="Bound">vc</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
In a moment we prove that `𝕍` is preserved when going from a greater
value to a lesser value: if `𝕍 v c` and `v' ⊑ v`, then `𝕍 v' c`.
This property, named `𝕍-sub`, is needed by the main lemma in
the case for the `sub` rule.

To prove `𝕍-sub`, we in turn need the following property concerning
values that are not greater than a function, that is, values that are
equivalent to `⊥`. In such cases, `𝕍 v (clos (ƛ N) γ')` is trivially true.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="not-above-fun-𝕍"></a><a id="10511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10511" class="Function">not-above-fun-𝕍</a> <a id="10527" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10529" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="10531" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10531" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10533" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10535" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4151" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="10540" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10542" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10542" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="10543" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10545" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10545" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="10548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2437" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="10558" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10542" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="10559" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10561" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10561" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="10563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10565" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10542" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3191" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10569" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="10571" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="10573" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="10575" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="10581" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10583" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="10585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4190" class="Function">above-fun</a> <a id="10595" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10531" class="Bound">v</a>
      <a id="10603" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
    <a id="10627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10631" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10531" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10633" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10639" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10642" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10561" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10643" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10645" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10545" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="10647" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="10649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10511" class="Function">not-above-fun-𝕍</a> <a id="10665" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4171" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a><a id="10667" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10669" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10669" class="Bound">af</a> <a id="10672" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10674" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#174" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>

    <a id="10790" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="10795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5795" class="Function">not-above-fun-⊔-inv</a> <a id="10815" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10783" class="Bound">af</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
The proofs of `𝕍-sub` and `𝔼-sub` are intertwined.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="sub-𝕍"></a><a id="10947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10947" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="10953" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10955" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="10957" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10957" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="10959" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2467" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="10965" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10967" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10967" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10969" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10969" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="10971" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10973" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10975" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10977" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10967" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10979" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10957" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="10981" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10983" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10969" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="10986" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4508" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="10988" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10967" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10990" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10992" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7244" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10994" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10969" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="10997" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10957" class="Bound">c</a>
<a id="sub-𝔼"></a><a id="10999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10999" class="Function">sub-𝔼</a> <a id="11005" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11007" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="11009" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11009" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11011" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11013" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2467" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="11017" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11019" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11019" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11021" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11021" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="11023" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11025" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11027" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7267" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="11029" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11019" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11031" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11009" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11033" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11035" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11021" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="11038" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4508" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="11040" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11019" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11042" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11044" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#7267" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="11046" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11021" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="11049" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11009" class="Bound">c</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
We prove `𝕍-sub` by case analysis on the closure's term, to dispatch the
cases for variables and application. We then proceed by induction on
`v' ⊑ v`. We describe each case below.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="11242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10947" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="11248" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="11254" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4330" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="11257" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11257" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11258" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11260" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11260" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="11261" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11263" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11264" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11264" class="Bound">v</a><a id="11265" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11267" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="11270" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11270" class="Bound">lt</a>
<a id="11273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10947" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="11279" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="11285" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11286" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11286" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="11288" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="11290" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11290" class="Bound">M</a><a id="11291" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11293" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11293" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="11294" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11296" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="11299" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#11299" class="Bound">lt</a>

<a id="12893" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="12897" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12899" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Sum.Base.html#687" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="12904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12904" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="12908" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12910" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.html#294" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="12917" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12918" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#809" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="12932" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#12904" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="12936" class="Bound">naf3</a><a id="12940" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
* Case `⊑-bot`. We immediately have `𝕍 ⊥ (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `⊑-conj-L`.

        v₁' ⊑ v     v₂' ⊑ v
        -------------------
        (v₁' ⊔ v₂') ⊑ v

  The induction hypotheses gives us `𝕍 v₁' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`
  and `𝕍 v₂' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`, which is all we need for this case.

* Case `⊑-conj-R1`.

        v' ⊑ v₁
        -------------
        v' ⊑ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)

  The induction hypothesis gives us `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `⊑-conj-R2`.

        v' ⊑ v₂
        -------------
        v' ⊑ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)

  Again, the induction hypothesis gives us `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `⊑-trans`.

        v' ⊑ v₂   v₂ ⊑ v
        -----------------
             v' ⊑ v

  The induction hypothesis for `v₂ ⊑ v` gives us
  `𝕍 v₂ (clos (ƛ N) γ)`. We apply the induction hypothesis
  for `v' ⊑ v₂` to conclude that `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `⊑-dist`. This case  is the most difficult. We have

        𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ)
        𝕍 (v ↦ w') (clos (ƛ N) γ)

  and need to show that

        𝕍 (v ↦ (w ⊔ w')) (clos (ƛ N) γ)

  Let `c` be an arbtrary closure such that `𝔼 v c`.
  Assume `w ⊔ w'` is greater than a function.
  Unfortunately, this does not mean that both `w` and `w'`
  are above functions. But thanks to the lemma `above-fun-⊔`,
  we know that at least one of them is greater than a function.

  * Suppose both of them are greater than a function.  Then we have
    `γ ⊢ N ⇓ clos L δ` and `𝕍 w (clos L δ)`.  We also have `γ ⊢ N ⇓ c₃` and
    `𝕍 w' c₃`.  Because the big-step semantics is deterministic, we have
    `c₃ ≡ clos L δ`. Also, from `𝕍 w (clos L δ)` we know that `L ≡ ƛ N'`
    for some `N'`. We conclude that `𝕍 (w ⊔ w') (clos (ƛ N') δ)`.

  * Suppose one of them is greater than a function and the other is
    not: say `above-fun w` and `¬ above-fun w'`. Then from
    `𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ)`
    we have `γ ⊢ N ⇓ clos L γ₁` and `𝕍 w (clos L γ₁)`. From this we have
    `L ≡ ƛ N'` for some `N'`. Meanwhile, from `¬ above-fun w'` we have
    `𝕍 w' (clos L γ₁)`. We conclude that
    `𝕍 (w ⊔ w') (clos (ƛ N') γ₁)`.


The proof of `sub-𝔼` is direct and explained below.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="15054" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10999" class="Function">sub-𝔼</a> <a id="15060" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="15066" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15066" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="15068" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15068" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="15069" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15071" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15072" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15072" class="Bound">v</a><a id="15073" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15075" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15076" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15076" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="15078" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15080" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15080" class="Bound">𝔼v</a> <a id="15083" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15083" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="15088" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15088" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a>
    <a id="15096" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="15101" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15080" class="Bound">𝔼v</a> <a id="15104" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15105" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4361" class="Function">above-fun-⊑</a> <a id="15117" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15088" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="15121" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15083" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a><a id="15125" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15127" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="15131" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="15133" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15135" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="15137" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15139" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15141" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15141" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="15145" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15147" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15147" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="15150" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15152" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15154" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="15162" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15135" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="15166" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15168" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15170" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15141" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="15174" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15176" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10947" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="15182" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#15147" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="15185" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="15190" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15192" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
From `above-fun v'` and `v' ⊑ v` we have `above-fun v`.  Then with `𝔼 v c` we
obtain a closure `c` such that `γ ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v c`. We conclude with an
application of `sub-𝕍` with `v' ⊑ v` to show `𝕍 v' c`.


## Programs with function denotation terminate via call-by-name

The main lemma proves that if a term has a denotation that is above a
function, then it terminates via call-by-name. More formally, if
`γ ⊢ M ↓ v` and `𝔾 γ γ'`, then `𝔼 v (clos M γ')`. The proof is by
induction on the derivation of `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` we discuss each case below.

The following lemma, kth-x, is used in the case for the `var` rule.
