    <a id="17896" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="17901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4907" class="Function">above-fun-⊔</a> <a id="17913" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#17866" class="Bound">fv12</a>
<a id="17918" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="17922" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="17924" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Sum.Base.html#662" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="17929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17929" class="Bound">fv1</a> <a id="17933" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17935" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.html#294" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="17942" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17943" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#809" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="17957" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#17929" class="Bound">fv1</a> <a id="17961" class="Bound">nfv1</a><a id="17965" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17967" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="17971" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="17973" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Sum.Base.html#687" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="17978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17978" class="Bound">fv2</a> <a id="17982" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17984" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.html#294" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="17991" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17992" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#809" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="18006" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#17978" class="Bound">fv2</a> <a id="18010" class="Bound">nfv2</a><a id="18014" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#16046" class="Function">↓→𝔼</a> <a id="18020" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18021" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18021" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="18022" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18024" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18025" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18025" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="18026" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18028" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18029" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18029" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="18031" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18033" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18034" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18034" class="Bound">M</a><a id="18035" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18037" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18038" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18038" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="18040" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18042" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18042" class="Bound">𝔾γγ&#39;</a> <a id="18047" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#9891" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a><a id="18051" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18052" class="Argument">v</a> <a id="18054" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18056" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18056" class="Bound">v</a><a id="18057" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18059" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18059" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="18061" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18061" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a><a id="18065" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18067" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18067" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a>
    <a id="18075" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="18080" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#16046" class="Function">↓→𝔼</a> <a id="18084" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18085" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18021" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="18086" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18088" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18089" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18025" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="18090" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18092" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18093" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18029" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="18095" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18097" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18098" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18034" class="Bound">M</a><a id="18099" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18101" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18042" class="Bound">𝔾γγ&#39;</a> <a id="18106" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18059" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="18108" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18109" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#4361" class="Function">above-fun-⊑</a> <a id="18121" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18067" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="18125" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18061" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a><a id="18129" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18131" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="18135" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="18137" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18139" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18139" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="18141" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18143" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18145" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18145" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="18149" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18151" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18151" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="18154" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="18156" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="18158" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="18166" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18139" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="18170" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18172" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18174" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18145" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="18178" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18180" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#10947" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="18186" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#18151" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="18189" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="18194" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="18196" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
* Case `var`. Looking up `x` in `γ'` yields some closure, `clos M' δ`,
  and from `𝔾 γ γ'` we have `𝔼 (γ x) (clos M' δ)`. With the premise
  `above-fun (γ x)`, we obtain a closure `c` such that `δ ⊢ M' ⇓ c`
  and `𝕍 (γ x) c`. To conclude `γ' ⊢ x ⇓ c` via `⇓-var`, we
  need `γ' x ≡ clos M' δ`, which is obvious, but it requires some
  Agda shananigans via the `kth-x` lemma to get our hands on it.

* Case `↦-elim`. We have `γ ⊢ L · M ↓ v`.
  The induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ L ↓ v₁ ↦ v`
  gives us `γ' ⊢ L ⇓ clos L' δ` and `𝕍 v (clos L' δ)`.
  Of course, `L' ≡ ƛ N` for some `N`.
  By the induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁`,
  we have `𝔼 v₁ (clos M γ')`.
  Together with the premise `above-fun v` and `𝕍 v (clos L' δ)`,
  we obtain a closure `c'` such that `δ ⊢ N ⇓ c'` and `𝕍 v c'`.
  We conclude that `γ' ⊢ L · M ⇓ c'` by rule `⇓-app`.

* Case `↦-intro`. We have `γ ⊢ ƛ N ↓ v ↦ w`.
  We immediately have `γ' ⊢ ƛ M ⇓ clos (ƛ M) γ'` by rule `⇓-lam`.
  But we also need to prove `𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ')`.
  Let `c` by an arbitrary closure such that `𝔼 v c`.
  Suppose `v'` is greater than a function value.
  We need to show that `γ' , c ⊢ N ⇓ c'` and `𝕍 v' c'` for some `c'`.
  We prove this by the induction hypothesis for `γ , v ⊢ N ↓ v'`
  but we must first show that `𝔾 (γ , v) (γ' , c)`. We prove
  that by the lemma `𝔾-ext`, using facts `𝔾 γ γ'` and `𝔼 v c`.

* Case `⊥-intro`. We have the premise `above-fun ⊥`, but that's impossible.

* Case `⊔-intro`. We have `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)` and `above-fun (v₁ ⊔ v₂)`
  and need to show `γ' ⊢ M ↓ c` and `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) c` for some `c`.
  Again, by `above-fun-⊔`, at least one of `v₁` or `v₂` is greater than
  a function.

  * Suppose both `v₁` and `v₂` are greater than a function value.
    By the induction hypotheses for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁` and `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₂`
    we have `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c₁`, `𝕍 v₁ c₁`, `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c₂`, and `𝕍 v₂ c₂`
    for some `c₁` and `c₂`. Because `⇓` is deterministic, we have `c₂ ≡ c₁`.
    Then by `𝕍⊔-intro` we conclude that `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) c₁`.

  * Without loss of generality, suppose `v₁` is greater than a function
    value but `v₂` is not.  By the induction hypotheses for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁`,
    and using `𝕍→WHNF`, we have `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N) γ₁`
    and `𝕍 v₁ (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`.
    Then because `v₂` is not greater than a function, we also have
    `𝕍 v₂ (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`. We conclude that `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`.

* Case `sub`. We have `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, `v' ⊑ v`, and `above-fun v'`.
  We need to show that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v' c` for some `c`.
  We have `above-fun v` by `above-fun-⊑`,
  so the induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` gives us a closure `c`
  such that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v c`. We conclude that `𝕍 v' c` by `sub-𝕍`.


## Proof of denotational adequacy

From the main lemma we can directly show that `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)` implies
that `M` big-steps to a lambda, i.e., `∅ ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) γ`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="↓→⇓"></a><a id="21083" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21083" class="Function">↓→⇓</a> <a id="21087" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21089" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="21091" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21091" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="21093" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21095" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3175" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="21097" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="21099" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="21100" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21102" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21102" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="21104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21106" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#3175" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="21108" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#3191" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="21110" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="21112" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="21114" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="21115" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="21118" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="21121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19666" class="Function">ℰ</a> <a id="21123" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21091" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="21125" href="plfa.part3.Denotational.html#19848" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="21127" href="plfa.part3.Denotational.html#19666" class="Function">ℰ</a> <a id="21129" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21130" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="21132" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21102" class="Bound">N</a><a id="21133" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="21412" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="21416" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="21418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="21421" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21422" class="Argument">N</a> <a id="21424" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21426" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21426" class="Bound">N′</a><a id="21428" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21430" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="21436" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="21438" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="21440" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="21442" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="21444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21426" class="Bound">N′</a> <a id="21447" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="21449" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="21451" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="21453" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="21455" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="21459" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>  <a id="21462" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="21464" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The proof goes as follows. We derive `∅ ⊢ ƛ N ↓ ⊥ ↦ ⊥` and
then `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)` gives us `∅ ⊢ M ↓ ⊥ ↦ ⊥`. We conclude
by applying the main lemma to obtain `∅ ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) γ`
for some `N′` and `γ`.

Now to prove the adequacy property. We apply the above
lemma to obtain `∅ ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) γ` and then
apply `cbn→reduce` to conclude.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="adequacy"></a><a id="21815" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21815" class="Function">adequacy</a> <a id="21824" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21826" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="21828" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21828" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="21830" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21832" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3175" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="21834" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="21836" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="21837" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21839" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21839" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="21841" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21843" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#3175" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="21845" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#3191" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="21847" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="21849" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="21851" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="21852" class="Symbol">}</a>
   <a id="21857" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="21860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#19666" class="Function">ℰ</a> <a id="21862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21828" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="21864" href="plfa.part3.Denotational.html#19848" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="21866" href="plfa.part3.Denotational.html#19666" class="Function">ℰ</a> <a id="21868" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="21871" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21839" class="Bound">N</a><a id="21872" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="21877" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21879" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="21882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21882" class="Bound">N′</a> <a id="21885" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="21887" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3175" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="21890" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#3191" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="21892" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="21894" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="21896" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="21897" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21899" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">]</a>
     <a id="21906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21828" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="21909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#11068" class="Datatype Operator">—↠</a> <a id="21912" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="21914" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21882" class="Bound">N′</a><a id="21916" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="21992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#12205" class="Function">cbn→reduce</a> <a id="22003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21977" class="Bound">M⇓</a>

## Call-by-name is equivalent to beta reduction

As promised, we return to the question of whether call-by-name
evaluation is equivalent to beta reduction. In chapter
[BigStep]({{ site.baseurl }}/BigStep/) we established the forward
direction: that if call-by-name produces a result, then the program
beta reduces to a lambda abstraction (`cbn→reduce`).  We now prove the backward
direction of the if-and-only-if, leveraging our results about the
denotational semantics.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="reduce→cbn"></a><a id="22487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22487" class="Function">reduce→cbn</a> <a id="22498" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22500" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22502" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22503" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#22503" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22505" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3175" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22509" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22511" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="22512" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22514" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22515" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#22515" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="22517" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22519" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#3175" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22521" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#3191" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="22523" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="22525" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4294" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22527" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#2888" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="22528" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="22541" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22543" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22503" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#11068" class="Datatype Operator">—↠</a> <a id="22548" href="plfa.part2.Untyped.html#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22550" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#22515" class="Bound">N</a>
           <a id="22563" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22565" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="22568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22568" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="22570" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="22572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3153" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="22580" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#911"              <a id="22634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/BigStep.md %}{% raw %}#2650" class="Function">∅&#39;</a> <a id="22637" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#3021" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22503" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22641" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#3021" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="22643" href="plfa.part2.BigStep.html#2486" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="22648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4382" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22651" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#22585" class="Bound">N′</a><a id="22653" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22655" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#22605" class="Bound">δ</a>
<a id="22657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22487" class="Function">reduce→cbn</a> <a id="22668" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#22668" class="Bound">M—↠ƛN</a> <a id="22674" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22676" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#21083" class="Function">↓→⇓</a> <a id="22680" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part3/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#23358" class="Function">soundness</a> <a id="22691" href="plfa.part3.Adequacy.html#22668" class="Bound">M—↠ƛN</a><a id="22696" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Suppose `M —↠ ƛ N`. Soundness of the denotational semantics gives us
`ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)`. Then by `↓→⇓` we conclude that
`∅' ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) δ` for some `N′` and `δ`.

Putting the two directions of the if-and-only-if together, we
establish that call-by-name evaluation is equivalent to beta reduction
in the following sense.
